I Get You Pro\r\n\r\nMost of us learn how to do our jobs effectively through a combination of training and trial and error. Learning the tactics for dealing with every type of person in all situations would be a task of gargantuan proportions, requiring almost super-human skills of memory retention and recall.\r\nThis is where I Get You Pro comes in…\r\nWhat does I Get You Pro do? \r\nI Get You Pro gives you situation-specific tactics for communicating with a particular individual – in a range of selling or managing contexts.\r\nIt helps you understand how people are different, and know what you need to do to communicate effectively with them, whatever you’re doing, to get the best outcome for you and for them.\r\nIs it a psychometric profiling tool? \r\nIt’s based on similar principles, but the big difference is that most psychometric profiling tools are designed for you to profile yourself, whereas I Get You Pro is a tool you use to profile other people.\r\nHow accurate is it? \r\nIt’s based on your perception of the person. Other people may have slightly different views. How you see someone is shaped by your knowledge and experience of them up to that point. If this is limited, your opinion will be less reliable than that of someone who knows them much better – but it’s a starting point, and any amount of insight is better than none at all.
